8The parent company in Hungen, Germany\nAll the business decisions of HAHN are taken here, just only half an hour away by car from Frankfurt’s International Airport; in terms of a qualitative and consumer-oriented corporate cultural philosophy. New, user-friendly products are developed here.  Progressive production technology for highest process quality and economically high volume is located here. All employees are trained to satisfy customer requirements all over the world.\nProduction in Güsten, Saxony-Anhalt, Germany\nThe rising demand for HAHN products in Eastern European countries made it  necessary to transfer partial production into a region near the border in order to  reduce logistical costs. \n3rd Production Plant in Novovolynsk (Ukraine)\nWith foundation of the 3rd plant in Eastern Europe, HAHN removed the manual  production from plant Hungen and Güsten to Novovolynsk. Custom-made and  wage-intensive products made this step necessary to be as one of the leading transformer producer further more competitive on the constantly growing market.HAHN Locations\nHungen/Hesse\nNovovolynsk (Ukraine)Güsten/Saxony-Anhalt\nwww.hahn-trafo.com 02/2016 Page 9HAHN Electronic Component Parts\nQuality awareness, product liability legislation and the growing demands of worldwide \nmarkets today make it necessary for equipment and appliance manufacturers to pass on these stringent requirements to their subcontractors and suppliers to ensure, that no component or assembly can become a critical weak spot. increasing requirements regarding the electro-\nmagnetic compatibility of network harmonics according  \nto DIN EN 61000 -3 has motivated HAHN to provide  \neconomical solutions for optimizing your products – whether by supplying alternative energy to networks or  \nby reducing harmonics caused by conversion.\nHAHN, with its vast experience and technical know-how, \nis now able to provide solutions in the form of a wide \nrange of customized coils. iron powder and ferrite.\nWhether it‘s a matter of designing a choke, optimizing  connections and wiring, assembly via foot angle or  \ntop-hat rail G 35, our vastly experienced team of highly ### Component Summary: BV2010129 from HAHN - ELEKTROBAU GMBH

#### Key Characteristics and Specifications:
- **Voltage Ratings**: Primary voltage up to 250 V.
- **Current Ratings**: Secondary current varies based on the specific model; for example, up to 350 mA for certain configurations.
- **Power Consumption**: Output power ranges from 0.35 VA to 0.5 VA.
- **Operating Temperature Range**: Rated for operation at a temperature class of ta 70 °C.
- **Package Type**: Frame size EI 20, suitable for printed circuit board (PCB) mounting.
- **Special Features**: 
  - Inherently short-circuit-proof.
  - Vacuum-encapsulated with dual chamber windings.
  - Self-extinguishing cast housing and sealing material.
  - Excellent temperature fluctuation resistance properties.
- **Moisture Sensitive Level**: Compliant with JEDEC J-STD-020E.

#### Description of the Component:
The BV2010129 is a printed circuit board transformer designed for low-power applications. It is characterized by its compact size and high efficiency, making it suitable for various electronic devices. The transformer is designed to provide electrical isolation and voltage transformation, ensuring safe operation in electronic circuits.

#### Typical Applications:
- **Power Supply**: Used in low-power applications such as household appliances, telecommunications, and small electronic devices.
- **Signal Processing**: Ideal for applications requiring signal isolation and transformation.
- **Control Systems**: Commonly used in control circuits where low voltage and current are needed.

This transformer is particularly beneficial in applications where space is limited, and high reliability is required, making it a versatile choice for manufacturers looking to integrate transformers into their products.
